<name>Mike H</name><date>1500680744891<//date><rating>1</rating>< review>
I own a bar in Brookings Oregon as well as several other businesses which use refrigeration. My normal refrigeration technician was ill and I decided to call Franks Refrigeration in Crescent City California. What a mistake that was!!!!
I am not one to write a negative review but in this case it is well deserved. I called Franks Office on 07/12/2017 because one of our ice machines was slowing down and the harvest times were off. I was informed that if I could be available between 10AM and 12PM that they had another appointment and would be already in Brookings and that the technician could swing by and have a look. The Technician showed up and immediately identified the problem as being a small internal screen filter approximately 6"x6" needed to be brushed off. A quick and easy fix constituting 4 screws one plug and the use of my shop vac and brush to clean off the screen allowing the proper air flow to the condenser coil. When I recieved the bill $309.30 including a $66.30 dollar "Trip Charge" I was less than happy. I called Franks several times and was unable to speak with anyone who could make any adjustments to the absorbent charges. I waited 8 days for the owner "Frank" to call me back with no such luck. Today I called again and spoke with a man who told me he would personally deliver my message to Frank. I received a call back from the owner "Frank" and I explained my position as to being told a technician would already be in my area and why I had a "Trip Charge" added to my bill? I also explained the nature of the problem and the quick fix that was required. I should add that we service our machines and filters on a regular basis and that this internal filter screen was apparently a common problem with the Manitowoc under counter ice machines. Frank told me he thought I was looking to get out of paying my bill and that the charges were justified. I got upset and said "its not ##cking right to tell someone one thing and than charge them another. Frank used this as his opportunity to end the call by hanging up on me, citing the fact that I used profanity. Guess what Frank I've now had my local refrigeration company here in Brookings inform me of your practices and your reputation. I must admit I had heard from other bar and restaurant owners that you had a bad reputation in Brookings and had my normal technician not been out sick I would never call a shiester like you. You ripped me off Frank and you are not even an honest enough guy to see the real issue here. I have rarely ever complained or made a fuss over poor service until today. 309 bucks for a fix that would have taken my regular technician an hour and cost me $75 buck !!!! Never again
I suggest anyone who ever reads this to call a different company and get an estimate.<//review>

The gas PRICES ARE A BIT HIGH and parking is a tight fit because the parking lot is EXTREMELY SMALL AND NO REAL BACK UP OR TURN AROUND ROOM. THIS PARKING LOT was not well planned and did not allow for the amount of traffic flow it receives hourly.

This 76 parking lot forces you to park in the street or open field behind the store which is RIDICULOUS when you stop and consider just how close to the 60 freeway East and West on and off ramps MAKES YOU THINK WHO IN THE PLANNING DEPARTMENT ok'd this and thought this was enough parking lot.

As for the store it is also small in size but is WELL STOCKED WITH GOODIES! The drinks are PLENTY TO CHOOSE FROM BOTH HOT AND COLD. And the store is always clean and neat and the people are very FRIENDLY and polite no matter the time of day you go.

I REALLY DO NOT STOP AT THIS 76 GAS STATION FOR GAS because the PRICE IS TOO HIGH but I stop regularly for drinks and the GAS STATION CHICKEN.

<user_id>104180822455294194097< /user_id>< Review>
Wow! I was hesitant to come here after seeing some of the reviews, but they accepted my medi-cal insurance and I was desperate, and I'm so glad I did!

They verified my insurance over the phone and made sure the Dr. On duty was able to diagnose the issue I was going in for, before I went in, which was really nice.

The reason I went was because I was convinced I had a kidney infection. I looked it up and had every symptom. My general doctor said I probably had Coronavirus and that's what they were going to test me for.... Not my kidney... , so I immediately left and found the Brentwood Urgent care. They saw me within 30 minutes, and the Dr immediately said, It sounds like a kidney infection and was shocked the other Dr would say otherwise. And of course, after tests, it was kidneys!

They gave me an injection of antibiotics and a prescription for antibiotics for the week and I was soooo happy that I had gotten a 2nd opinion! The whole office was so nice and efficient. I am shocked that anyone would give them a bad review! I will definitely be coming here from now on when I have an urgent issue!< /Review>

< Review>
Disappointed to be writing this review. Been there a handful of times, and it's always been better than other urgent cares in the area, but that isn't necessarily saying much. I went in last week and was told by the doctor that I only had a cold and to go home, take Tylenol and wait it out. I did so and actually began to feel better after a couple of days. But then the nasal congestion I was feeling returned and spread to my ear. The doctor said this might happen, so I called and inquired whether I would have to pay for a second visit since it is still within a week of my last visit. I was told that I would indeed have to pay again. Other urgent cares (such as one in Hollywood and another Downtown) offer a free return visit if symptoms persist within a week. Not Brentwood. Very disappointing. At this point, I'll wait and see. If I get worse, I'll try and see an ENT. An ENT would have a lower copay anyway. Never returning.< /Review>

< Review>
Its horrible. The people aren't very happy to help at all, they give you a rude look when you ask for something, and not at all welcoming. A few years ago they took away the magazine seating area, took away chairs, and patched up all the wall plugs to make sure nobody charges their phones or laptops. Barnes and Noble doesn't even give coupons. Its why competition is so important.

Borders always welcomed customers with friendly service, constantly gave 40% off coupons every week, and never acted as selfish as B&N has. I just get everything from Amazon now or go to the library nearby.

Highly recommend the Montclair mall B&N, they have more in stock, starbucks seating area, more inventory and they aren't greedy with letting people relax and read a book. Well worth the extra drive.</Review>
